        <article>
            The AMD <strong>Ryzen</strong> 3rd gen processors give you a huge boost in power over the previous generation. You&apos;ll get a faster CPU with more memory &#x2013; perfect for gaming, or just powering through huge work projects and creative tasks.<br> <br> The <strong>Ryzen 7 3800X</strong>&#xA0;also supports PCIe 4.0 connectivity. So you&apos;re futureproofed for the most advanced motherboards, graphics and storage. When it&apos;s time to upgrade your PC again &#x2013; your processor will still be ready to go.<br> <br> There&apos;s an RGB Wraith Prism cooler in the box too &#x2013; one less thing to worry about when you&apos;re building your PC.

                                            <p><strong>Get this delivered when it suits you</strong><br><br>We&#x2019;ll show you your current delivery options for this item in checkout. Subject to the time you order, and where you want delivery, these options will include:<br></p><ul><li><strong>FREE standard delivery</strong> in 3-5 working days</li><li><strong>Next day delivery or any following day</strong> between 8am &amp; 5pm <strong>(&#xA3;5.00)</strong></li><li><strong>Delivery in a timeslot of your choice </strong>next day or any following day <strong>(&#xA3;10.00)</strong></li></ul>  Please note: if we&#x2019;re out of stock of an item but getting more in, we indicate &#x2013; on listings pages and the product page &#x2013; how soon we can dispatch for delivery to you. In this case, please go ahead and order, and we&#x2019;ll contact you later to confirm an exact delivery date.<p></p><h4>Important update on our delivery service for small items</h4><p><strong>Our courier partners (DPD, Royal Mail and On the Dot) have all updated their delivery processes to take extra precautions due to Coronavirus (COVID-19). Please follow the below advice:</strong></p><p>1. Customers can use the DPD app to nominate a &#x2018;safe place&#x2019; for their delivery to be left if they do not want close contact.</p><p>For customers unable to use the DPD app, DPD is still able to offer a contact-free delivery, and will take a picture of the property and capture a proof of delivery name instead of capturing a customer signature.</p><p>2. Royal Mail is an unsigned service . Where Royal Mail needs to deliver a parcel, its teams will place the parcel at the customer&#x2019;s door. Having knocked on the door, the delivery teams will step aside to a safe distance while the item is retrieved. If the delivery cannot take place, Royal Mail will take the parcel to the local depot for collection by the customer.&#xA0; The parcel will be held for 18 days as per normal process.</p><p>3. For On the Dot, where a standard signature delivery is not possible, On the Dot will attempt to leave the parcel in a safe place and inform the customer of where the parcel has been placed.</p><p>To see the courier partner for your delivery, <strong>please check your dispatch confirmation email</strong> (which will also include your tracking reference).</p><h4>Availability Checker</h4>How and when can you get hold of your selections? This promise is in addition to your statutory rights.<br><br><h5>Items you&#x2019;ve opened</h5>Within 14 days of receiving <strong>an item you paid for online or on the phone</strong>, you can return it, even if you&#x2019;ve opened it. To receive a refund, you must:<br><br><ul><li>Let us know you plan to return the item within 14 days of delivery/collection</li><li>Physically return it within a further 14 days.</li></ul>The item must be returned in <strong>&#x2018;as new condition&#x2019;</strong> &#x2013; not used or installed, and in its original packaging. <a href="https://www.currys.co.uk/gbuk/returns-cancellations-1043-theme.html">More on returns and refunds.</a><br><br>

<script language="javascript" type="text/javascript" charset="utf-8">
/* Chat Launched Listener checker */

var chatLaunchedListener = {
       onChatLaunched:function(evt){

            if (evt.chatType == "POPUP")
            {
                var analyticsEvent = "event63"
            }
            else if (evt.chatType == "C2C")
            {
                var analyticsEvent = "event66"
            }

            if (analyticsEvent){
                s.events=analyticsEvent;
                s.linkTrackVars="events";
                s.linkTrackEvents=analyticsEvent;
                s.tl(true, "o", "Chat Interaction")
        }      
    }
};
/*Check if the chat window w2as engaged - triggered by customer*/
var chatEngagedListener = { 
    onChatEngagedEvent: function(evt){
        if (evt.chatType == "POPUP"){
            var analyticsEvent = "event64"
        }
        else if (evt.chatType == "C2C")
        {
            var analyticsEvent = "event67"
        }
        
        if (analyticsEvent){
            s.events=analyticsEvent;
            s.linkTrackVars="events";
            s.linkTrackEvents=analyticsEvent;
            s.tl(true, "o", "Chat Interaction")
        }
    }
};

var saleQualifiedListener = { 

    onSaleQualifiedEvent: function(evt){
        if (evt.chatType == "POPUP"){
            var analyticsEvent = "event65"
        }else if (evt.chatType == "C2C"){
            var analyticsEvent = "event68"
        }
        
        if (analyticsEvent){
            s.events=analyticsEvent;
            s.eVar68=evt.chatID;
            s.linkTrackVars="events,eVar68";
            s.linkTrackEvents=analyticsEvent;
            s.tl(true, "o", "Chat Interaction")
        }
    }
};
        

</script>

<script>
/* Register TC listeners */

if(typeof InqRegistry !== 'undefined') {
  InqRegistry.chatListeners.push(chatLaunchedListener);
  InqRegistry.saleListeners.push(saleQualifiedListener, chatEngagedListener);


} else {
  window.InqRegistry = {
    chatListeners:[chatLaunchedListener],
    saleListeners:[saleQualifiedListener,chatEngagedListener]
  }
}

</script>

<script language="javascript" type="text/javascript" charset="utf-8">

    function JSChainLoader(srclist, isRetry) {
        if (0 < srclist.length) {
            var src = srclist.shift();
            var script = document.createElement('script');
            script.onload = function(){JSChainLoader(srclist, false);};
            script.onreadystatechange = function(){JSChainLoader(srclist, false);};
            script.onerror = function(){
                if (false === isRetry) {
                    srclist.unshift(src);
                }
                JSChainLoader(srclist, true);
            };
            document.body.appendChild(script);
            script.src = src;
        }
    }

</script>

            The AMD <strong>Ryzen</strong> 3rd gen processors give you a huge boost in power over the previous generation. You&apos;ll get a faster CPU with more memory &#x2013; perfect for gaming, or just powering through huge work projects and creative tasks.<br> <br> The <strong>Ryzen 7 3800X</strong>&#xA0;also supports PCIe 4.0 connectivity. So you&apos;re futureproofed for the most advanced motherboards, graphics and storage. When it&apos;s time to upgrade your PC again &#x2013; your processor will still be ready to go.<br> <br> There&apos;s an RGB Wraith Prism cooler in the box too &#x2013; one less thing to worry about when you&apos;re building your PC.

                <div class="sep">
                                            <p><strong>Get this delivered when it suits you</strong><br><br>We&#x2019;ll show you your current delivery options for this item in checkout. Subject to the time you order, and where you want delivery, these options will include:<br></p><ul><li><strong>FREE standard delivery</strong> in 3-5 working days</li><li><strong>Next day delivery or any following day</strong> between 8am &amp; 5pm <strong>(&#xA3;5.00)</strong></li><li><strong>Delivery in a timeslot of your choice </strong>next day or any following day <strong>(&#xA3;10.00)</strong></li></ul>  Please note: if we&#x2019;re out of stock of an item but getting more in, we indicate &#x2013; on listings pages and the product page &#x2013; how soon we can dispatch for delivery to you. In this case, please go ahead and order, and we&#x2019;ll contact you later to confirm an exact delivery date.<p></p><h4>Important update on our delivery service for small items</h4><p><strong>Our courier partners (DPD, Royal Mail and On the Dot) have all updated their delivery processes to take extra precautions due to Coronavirus (COVID-19). Please follow the below advice:</strong></p><p>1. Customers can use the DPD app to nominate a &#x2018;safe place&#x2019; for their delivery to be left if they do not want close contact.</p><p>For customers unable to use the DPD app, DPD is still able to offer a contact-free delivery, and will take a picture of the property and capture a proof of delivery name instead of capturing a customer signature.</p><p>2. Royal Mail is an unsigned service . Where Royal Mail needs to deliver a parcel, its teams will place the parcel at the customer&#x2019;s door. Having knocked on the door, the delivery teams will step aside to a safe distance while the item is retrieved. If the delivery cannot take place, Royal Mail will take the parcel to the local depot for collection by the customer.&#xA0; The parcel will be held for 18 days as per normal process.</p><p>3. For On the Dot, where a standard signature delivery is not possible, On the Dot will attempt to leave the parcel in a safe place and inform the customer of where the parcel has been placed.</p><p>To see the courier partner for your delivery, <strong>please check your dispatch confirmation email</strong> (which will also include your tracking reference).</p><h4>Availability Checker</h4>How and when can you get hold of your selections? Finding out should be quick and easy, so with just a few clicks our Availability Checker shows you:<br><br><ul><li>Delivery dates, time-slots and prices</li><li>Local stores with stock you can collect from now</li><li>Local stores you can get items sent to for you to collect later</li></ul>To use our Availability Checker, simply:<br><br><ol><li>Enter a town or postcode in the box on the product page for an item you&#x2019;ve selected</li><li>Click on the magnifying glass</li><li>Review the delivery and collection options local to you &#x2013; just click on any one to add it to your basket</li></ol><h4>Stock updates</h4>Find something you want but it&#x2019;s not in stock? On the item&#x2019;s product page, simply click on &#x2018;Email me when back in stock&#x2019;, and let us have your email address. We&#x2019;ll let you know as soon as it&#x2019;s available again.<br><br><h4>Returns and refunds</h4>Whether an item you&#x2019;ve bought is faulty or damaged, or you&#x2019;ve changed your mind, it&#x2019;s easy to get a refund.<br><br><h5>Items you haven&#x2019;t opened</h5>Within 21 days of receiving <strong>an item you paid for online, on the phone, or in store</strong> you can return it for a full refund &#x2013; provided your purchase is still in its original and unopened packaging. This promise is in addition to your statutory rights.<br><br><h5>Items you&#x2019;ve opened</h5>Within 14 days of receiving <strong>an item you paid for online or on the phone</strong>, you can return it, even if you&#x2019;ve opened it. To receive a refund, you must:<br><br><ul><li>Let us know you plan to return the item within 14 days of delivery/collection</li><li>Physically return it within a further 14 days.</li></ul>The item must be returned in <strong>&#x2018;as new condition&#x2019;</strong> &#x2013; not used or installed, and in its original packaging. <a href="https://www.currys.co.uk/gbuk/returns-cancellations-1043-theme.html">More on returns and refunds.</a><br><br>

Here&#x2019;s how it works;<br><br><ul> <li>Once you&#x2019;ve had confirmation your order is ready to collect, drive to the store.</li> <li>When you&#x2019;ve arrived, click on the link in your confirmation email to let our team know.</li> <li>One of our colleagues will put your order in your car boot.</li></ul><br>Stores, including those which <strong>DO NOT</strong> have parking outside, can still offer a safe <strong>Walk Up</strong> service. Here&#x2019;s how it works;<br><br><ul> <li>Once you&#x2019;ve had confirmation your order is ready to collect, walk to store and head to the collection point.</li> <li>When you&#x2019;ve arrived, click on the link in your confirmation email to let our team know.</li> <li>You&#x2019;ll get a text when our colleague is preparing your order for collection.</li> <li>Please remember to keep 2 metres away from our colleagues and other customers.</li></ul><br>If the store already has stock of your item, you may be able to collect on the same day. <script language="javascript" type="text/javascript" charset="utf-8">
/* Chat Launched Listener checker */

var chatLaunchedListener = {
       onChatLaunched:function(evt){

            if (evt.chatType == "POPUP")
            {
                var analyticsEvent = "event63"
            }
            else if (evt.chatType == "C2C")
            {
                var analyticsEvent = "event66"
            }

            if (analyticsEvent){
                s.events=analyticsEvent;
                s.linkTrackVars="events";
                s.linkTrackEvents=analyticsEvent;
                s.tl(true, "o", "Chat Interaction")
        }      
    }
};
/*Check if the chat window w2as engaged - triggered by customer*/
var chatEngagedListener = { 
    onChatEngagedEvent: function(evt){
        if (evt.chatType == "POPUP"){
            var analyticsEvent = "event64"
        }
        else if (evt.chatType == "C2C")
        {
            var analyticsEvent = "event67"
        }
        
        if (analyticsEvent){
            s.events=analyticsEvent;
            s.linkTrackVars="events";
            s.linkTrackEvents=analyticsEvent;
            s.tl(true, "o", "Chat Interaction")
        }
    }
};

var saleQualifiedListener = { 

    onSaleQualifiedEvent: function(evt){
        if (evt.chatType == "POPUP"){
            var analyticsEvent = "event65"
        }else if (evt.chatType == "C2C"){
            var analyticsEvent = "event68"
        }
        
        if (analyticsEvent){
            s.events=analyticsEvent;
            s.eVar68=evt.chatID;
            s.linkTrackVars="events,eVar68";
            s.linkTrackEvents=analyticsEvent;
            s.tl(true, "o", "Chat Interaction")
        }
    }
};
        

</script>

<script>
/* Register TC listeners */

if(typeof InqRegistry !== 'undefined') {
  InqRegistry.chatListeners.push(chatLaunchedListener);
  InqRegistry.saleListeners.push(saleQualifiedListener, chatEngagedListener);


} else {
  window.InqRegistry = {
    chatListeners:[chatLaunchedListener],
    saleListeners:[saleQualifiedListener,chatEngagedListener]
  }
}

</script>


<!-- Webchat: chainloading: (remote) Navigation Variables, TouchCommerce Global JS Tag -->
<script language="javascript" type="text/javascript" charset="utf-8">

    function JSChainLoader(srclist, isRetry) {
        if (0 < srclist.length) {
            var src = srclist.shift();
            var script = document.createElement('script');
            script.onload = function(){JSChainLoader(srclist, false);};
            script.onreadystatechange = function(){JSChainLoader(srclist, false);};
            script.onerror = function(){
                if (false === isRetry) {
                    srclist.unshift(src);
                }
                JSChainLoader(srclist, true);
            };
            document.body.appendChild(script);
            script.src = src;
        }
    }

</script>
<!-- WebChat: Navigation Variables -->
<script language="javascript" type="text/javascript" charset="utf-8">
(function() {
    var standardMode = !!window.addEventListener;
    var eventMethod = standardMode? 'addEventListener' : 'attachEvent';
    var eventName = standardMode? 'load' : 'onload';
    window[eventMethod](eventName, function() {
        window.jQuery.ajax({
            method : 'GET', 
            url : 'https://www.currys.co.uk/gb/uk/webchat_navigation/ajax.html',
                        data: 'productid=10194807',
                        dataType: 'json',
            success: function(data) {
                    window.inqCustData = data;
                    JSChainLoader(['https://dixons.inq.com/chatskins/launch/inqChatLaunch10004048.js']);
            },
            error: function() {
                    JSChainLoader(['https://dixons.inq.com/chatskins/launch/inqChatLaunch10004048.js']);
            }
        });
        
    });
})();
</script>
